# Policy Bot - UI Wireframes

## Overview

This document contains ASCII wireframes for all user interfaces in the Policy Bot application.

---

## 7. Admin Dashboard

The admin dashboard uses a tabbed interface with seven sections: Dashboard, Documents, Categories, Users, Data Sources, Function APIs, and Settings.

### Upload Document Modal (Tabbed Interface)

The admin upload modal now features a tabbed interface allowing both file uploads and direct text content entry.

```
Legend:
[Admin] = Red badge
[SuperUser] = Purple badge (clickable - opens edit role)
[User] = Blue badge (clickable - opens edit role)
[âš™] = Manage subscriptions/assignments
[ğŸ—‘] = Delete user (disabled for own account)
Categories = Subscribed categories (users) or assigned categories (superusers)
```

```
Legend:
[Active] = Blue badge (currently selected model)
[â—] = Green badge (provider connected)
[!] = Yellow badge (configured but unavailable)
[â—‹] = Gray badge (not configured)
```

```
Available icons:
- government (Landmark) - Government/official
- operations (Settings) - Operations/config
- finance (DollarSign) - Finance/money
- kpi (BarChart3) - KPI/metrics
- logs (FileText) - Logs/documents
- data (Database) - Data/storage
- monitoring (Activity) - Monitoring/health
- architecture (Layers) - Architecture/systems
- internet (Globe) - Internet/web
- systems (Server) - Systems/servers
- policy (ScrollText) - Policy/rules (default)
```

### Dynamic Chat Header


## 8. Super User Dashboard

Super users have a dedicated dashboard to manage documents and users in their assigned categories.

```
Legend:
[HR] = Orange category badge
[Ready] = Green status badge
[Process] = Yellow status badge (processing)
[ğŸ—‘] = Delete (only visible for documents uploaded by this super user)
```

### Upload Document Modal (Super User - Tabbed Interface)

Super users have a similar tabbed interface but with restricted options (single category, no global flag).

## 9. Category Selector Component

The Category Selector allows users to filter which document categories to search in for their queries.

### Chat Thread Category Selector

## Component Specifications

### Colors (Tailwind Classes)
| Element | Light Mode | Dark Mode (Future) |
|---------|------------|-------------------|
| Primary | `blue-600` | `blue-400` |
| Background | `gray-50` | `gray-900` |
| User Bubble | `blue-600` | `blue-500` |
| Assistant Bubble | `gray-100` | `gray-800` |
| Text Primary | `gray-900` | `gray-100` |
| Text Secondary | `gray-500` | `gray-400` |
| Border | `gray-200` | `gray-700` |
| Error | `red-500` | `red-400` |
| Success | `green-500` | `green-400` |

### Role Badge Colors
| Role | Background | Text |
|------|------------|------|
| Admin | `red-100` | `red-800` |
| SuperUser | `purple-100` | `purple-800` |
| User | `blue-100` | `blue-800` |

### Category Badge Colors
| Type | Background | Text |
|------|------------|------|
| Global | `green-100` | `green-800` |
| Specific | `blue-100` | `blue-800` |

### Status Badge Colors
| Status | Background | Text |
|--------|------------|------|
| Active | `green-100` | `green-800` |
| Paused | `yellow-100` | `yellow-800` |
| Processing | `blue-100` | `blue-800` |
| Error | `red-100` | `red-800` |

### Provider Status Badge Colors
| Status | Background | Text | Indicator |
|--------|------------|------|-----------|
| Connected | `green-100` | `green-800` | Green dot |
| Configured (unavailable) | `yellow-100` | `yellow-800` | Yellow dot |
| Not configured | `gray-100` | `gray-600` | Gray dot |

### Spacing
- Sidebar width: `280px` (desktop)
- Chat padding: `16px`
- Message gap: `16px`
- Border radius: `8px` (cards), `16px` (bubbles)

### Typography
- Headings: `font-semibold`
- Body: `text-sm` to `text-base`
- Timestamps: `text-xs text-gray-500`
